        network-queue "nqNetwork" create
            description "Network Egress Queue"
            queue 1 create
                rate 100 cir 20
                mbs 100
                cbs 20
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 2 best-effort create
                rate 100 cir 50
                cbs 50
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 3 expedite create
                rate 100 cir 30
                cbs 30
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 9 multipoint create
                mbs 50
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 11 multipoint best-effort create
                cbs 20
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 12 multipoint best-effort create
                rate 100 cir 50
                cbs 50
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 13 multipoint expedite create
                rate 100 cir 30
                cbs 30
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            fc be create
                multicast-queue 11
                queue 1
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 1
                exit
            exit
            fc ef create
                multicast-queue 12
                queue 2
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 6
                exit
            exit
            fc h2 create
                multicast-queue 13
                queue 3
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 5
                exit
            exit
        exit
        slope-policy "spDrop" create
            description "drop profile"
            high-slope
                start-avg 80
                max-avg 95
                max-prob 10
                no shutdown
            exit
            low-slope
                start-avg 30
                max-avg 95
                max-prob 20
                no shutdown
            exit
            time-average-factor 9
        exit
    exit
